 ek media report main buudhvaar ko iskaa khulaasa kiya gaya
 Dawn News quoted diplomatic observers as saying that Pakistan is exploring the possibility of building a larger South Asian Economic Organization in the cut of India's "dominance" in the eight-member South Asian Association for Regional Cooperation (SAARC)
